Diplomatic Activities Still Underway in Geneva, No Difficulty for Various Countries to Participate in Sanctions 9

(Geneva) A certain key figure in the British delegation recently stated to a Havas News Agency reporter, "Rumors that diplomatic activities have now moved from Geneva to London or Paris are incorrect. The Economic Sanctions Committee has not encountered any significant resistance in drafting the sanctions plan. Firstly, no country refuses to participate in the sanctions. Although countries such as Poland and Switzerland have reluctantly提出some reservations, they still support the sanctions in principle. Secondly, the British side has not only not advocated strict implementation of sanctions but has also requested the committee to consider various special circumstances. Thirdly, France has consistently supported the British viewpoint. Therefore, the future is very promising." Furthermore, according to sources within the League of Nations, even if the compensation and mutual assistance system stipulated in Article 16 of the Covenant is extremely complex, the sanctions work should not be delayed or harmed as a result. Regarding this, responsible individuals claim that the Economic Mutual Assistance Committee will likely adopt the proposal of Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu, namely that all countries participating in the sanctions should strive to develop their mutual trade. When redistributing markets in the future, countries that have suffered the greatest losses due to faithfully fulfilling collective measures should receive greater preferential treatment. Conversely, countries that do not implement sanctions should not enjoy these preferences. Reliable sources claim that if this approach is used to resolve the issue, it will not be difficult for countries to gradually restore free trade policies. (Havas News Agency, 17th)

(Geneva) The general debate of the Economic Mutual Assistance Committee has concluded. It has now been decided to adopt the following measures: (1) Establish a compensation system to provide countries that suffer losses from participating in sanctions with alternative trade outlets to offset those losses. (2) Establish a credit system to allow countries in need of financial assistance to obtain loans. In addition, measures have been discussed to address those who do not participate in sanctions but individually offer goods for sale to Italy to profit from the opportunity. The committee has now appointed representatives from France, Spain, Britain, Romania, the Soviet Union, Yugoslavia, and Italy as drafting committee members to immediately begin drafting a concrete plan for economic mutual assistance. (Havas News Agency, 17th)

(London) The United Kingdom exports the most coal to France. Aside from France, Italy is the second-largest customer. Therefore, if economic sanctions are imposed on Italy, the British coal mining regions will inevitably be greatly affected. This is a matter of considerable concern to British officials. After detailed research by various cabinet departments, it was pointed out that if British coal exports to Italy are halted, the losses incurred cannot be compensated. In 1934, Italy purchased a total of 4.7 million tons of coal from the United Kingdom, valued at £3.5 million, accounting for one-eighth of the total British coal exports. Aside from France, which purchases £7 million worth of British coal annually, no other country purchases as much as Italy. Therefore, some key figures believe that the United Kingdom's imposition of sanctions on Italy is definitely not in the UK's own interests, as can be seen from this perspective. Furthermore, officials believe that this loss is impossible to compensate for. In Europe, the amount of coal purchased by various European countries cannot be changed. Countries such as the Baltic states and Spain purchase most of their required coal from the United Kingdom, and this cannot be increased. The amount of coal purchased by Germany, France, Belgium, and the Netherlands also cannot be changed. As for Poland, it is not a customer but instead exports coal, competing with the United Kingdom. In addition, the countries of the Balkan Peninsula do not require much coal. The only way to seek compensation is to increase sales to Greece or countries outside Europe, such as Egypt, to offset the loss of the Italian market, which is extremely difficult. (Havas News Agency, 18th)

The cabinet reshuffle has placed all key government positions under the control of the Heimwehr. It is expected that the new cabinet's pro-Italian stance will be even stronger than before. Although the country claims to be peaceful, the Vienna Heimwehr and the Farmers' League are secretly jealous of Starhemberg. He has admitted that his goal is to restore the Habsburg monarchy. He associated with Hitler in his early years and was responsible for studying Italian Fascism, thus harboring the ambition to form his own army. Therefore, he founded the paramilitary Heimwehr, whose organization is very similar to Germany's National Socialist Party and Mussolini's Blackshirts. (Reuters, 18th)

(Vienna) Chancellor Schuschnigg and the entire cabinet resigned today. However, the cabinet was soon successfully reorganized. In the new cabinet, Interior Minister and Director General of Public Security Fey was removed and replaced by Baron Wölfel, leader of the national Heimwehr. Fey was the leader of the Vienna Heimwehr. Today's cabinet resignation was the result of the Heimwehr in southern Austria threatening the capital. This change ended with Baron Wolf succeeded him as Minister of the Interior. The inside story is that Chancellor Schuschnigg and Heimwehr leader Prince Starhemberg united to exclude radical elements in the Heimwehr. After the reorganization, Austria's foreign policy remains conservatively pro-Italian. Schuschnigg remains Chancellor. In addition to Fey, Justice Minister Karwinsky and Agriculture Minister Reither have also been excluded, and replaced by two members of the Socialist Party close to Prince Starhemberg and two conservative leaders in the Heimwehr. One of them is a cabinet minister without portfolio. Today, rumors circulated that Fey had plotted a coup, which failed due to the cabinet change. However, this claim could not be confirmed. Prince Starhemberg announced that the volunteer army would be reorganized by merging with the original organization and removing all unqualified members. He also said, "I pledge to fulfill my responsibility to keep the United States from being caught up in the conflicts that are now pushing us into the path of war. This figure includes silver purchased before September 27th. The Treasury Department report also stated that the purchased silver can be categorized as follows: 48,000,000 ounces of newly mined silver, 122,000,000 ounces of silver coins and bars, and 290,000,000 ounces of silver purchased from around the world under the Silver Purchase Act. Current Commentary

Military Situation of British-Italian Confrontation 22

— Yi

Since the outbreak of the Italian-Abyssinian War, the British government has, in its diplomatic efforts, advocated strict sanctions against Italy. It has, within a very short period, enabled the League of Nations to successively pass three concrete proposals regarding economic sanctions. In military terms, it concentrated the main force of its navy in the Mediterranean to prepare for contingencies. According to recent news, the British military authorities have again transferred five battleships and ten destroyers to the Mediterranean and held a naval exercise of a demonstrative nature on the evening of the 15th. At the same time, British ships from the West Indies were requisitioned to return to Europe to aid in defense. Although French Premier Laval has recently been strongly urging the British authorities to reduce their military presence in the Mediterranean in order to ease the crisis of war, the British government has ultimately not heeded his advice. A semi-official British spokesman has publicly stated in recent days that the United Kingdom may be forced to block Italian coasts, the Suez Canal, and the mouths of the Red Sea. Furthermore, yesterday's London dispatch had a 可　credible rumor that Mussolini had decided to strike first and initiate armed conflict with the United Kingdom. Since the European War, the treacherousness of the Mediterranean situation has rarely exceeded what it is today.

The increasingly expansionist military strength of Fascist Italy in recent years was, in fact, fostered by the United Kingdom. Its greed for Abyssinia was also, in fact, induced by the United Kingdom. The UK originally wanted to use Italy's power to suppress France and Germany. Now that Italy has actually launched an attack on Abyssinia, the United Kingdom has turned against Italy. The reason for this is that once Mussolini's eastern expedition succeeds, it would pose a serious threat to the vast and scattered British Empire on its main route connecting to the Far East. Please, based on this meaning, discuss the military situation of the two countries in the Mediterranean.

First, regarding the terrain, if the United Kingdom wants to maintain the route through Suez, it must maintain its military posture controlling the Mediterranean. The eastern and western gateways of the Mediterranean, Port Said and Gibraltar, are both under British control and have fortresses. Malta in the center also has a naval port built with a large navy stationed there. The above three places have formed a solid military communication line. In addition, the United Kingdom also pays attention to the defense of the Suez Canal. A Famagusta military port has been built on the island of Cyprus, forming a triangular defense line with Port Said and Jaffa in Palestine. Today, the British Empire's layout to control the Mediterranean is roughly like this. However, on the Italian side, since occupying Libya in 1912, a military port has been built in Tripoli. It has acquired a military base on the southern shore of the Mediterranean. The Dodecanese Islands opposite Asia Minor were also occupied by Italy in 1912. The military ports built by Italy on its islands of Rhodes and Leros in recent years not only threaten the southern coast of Turkey, but also force the British navy in the eastern Mediterranean to be more vigilant. The Italian navy stationed on the two islands can launch attacks on the British navy's triangular defense line at any time.

Secondly, regarding strength, the progress of world air force tactics in recent years is sufficient to reduce the power of the navy. This is a consensus among military experts. Italy's large air force today has the potential to shake the two fortresses of Malta and Gibraltar. Even the British military expert Strappo Borghi does not deny this. Let us put aside the air force for the moment and only compare the naval strength of the two countries. According to an article by British naval expert Paivat published in the London Daily News in August, Italy's newly built cruisers and existing submarines are considered more elite than those of the United Kingdom. The dreadnoughts under construction are the largest in the world. However, Italy's naval modernization plan has not yet been completed, and the navy that has received rigorous training is only 85,000 strong. Whether it has the ability to control the United Kingdom's eastern route is still difficult to say. According to an investigation by the British naval authorities, Italian warships in the Mediterranean have a total displacement of 284,734 tons, while the total displacement of the British Empire's standing fleet in the Mediterranean is only 200,000 tons. If something happens in the Mediterranean, the United Kingdom can still requisition its home fleet and Far East fleet. But judging from the above situation, unless it truly cooperates with France, the United Kingdom's sole strength may still be difficult to overwhelm Italy.

In summary, the United Kingdom's position in the Mediterranean today is far from comparable to what it was in the past. When Mussolini had a border dispute with Greece in 1923 and attempted to occupy Corfu Island, he was still wary of British intervention. Today, the situation in the Mediterranean is such that Italy has already dispatched 200,000 to 300,000 troops, along with countless airplanes, tanks, and all military supplies, to the border of Abyssinia, spending more than 200 million lire. At this moment, when the Fascist spirit is unleashed and difficult to restrain, seeking a peaceful resolution to the British-Italian conflict is certainly far less easy than the 1923 incident.

Legislative Yuan Revises and Passes Three Railway Regulations; Principles of the Draft Constitution Under Study 40

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan held its 33rd meeting on the morning of the 18th, attended by 66 members including Lin Bin. Sun Ke chaired the meeting, and Secretary-General Liang Han Cao was also present. Items for discussion: (1) Private Railway Regulations; (2) Public Railway Regulations. Resolution: Both of the above regulations were revised and passed in accordance with the review report of seven members including Ma Yinchu. (3) Dedicated Railway Regulations. Resolution: Passed according to the review results of the Economic, Legal, and Financial Committees. Among the three regulations, the issue of issuing company bonds in the Private Railway Regulations caused heated debate among the members. As a result, according to the chairman's proposal, the amount of company bonds issued by private railway companies shall not exceed the total value of existing assets, except when necessary to complete the construction of the railway line. (Central News Agency Telegram, 18th)

(Nanjing) The main points of the three railway regulations passed by the Legislative Yuan on the 18th are as follows: (1) The Private Railway Regulations consist of nine chapters, including general provisions, establishment, organization, engineering, operation, finance, purchase, penalties, and supplementary provisions, totaling 73 articles. These regulations apply to Chinese citizens who organize companies with capital to build railways for the purpose of transporting passengers and goods. Private railways may include government shares but not foreign shares, nor may they borrow foreign debt, unless specially permitted. Private railways may raise company bonds, but the amount of debt shall not exceed the total value of existing assets, except when necessary to complete the construction of the railway line. The operating period for private railways is limited to 30 years. After the expiration of the period, if the government does not purchase them at a price, the right to operate may be extended for another ten years. (2) The Public Railway Regulations consist of 36 articles. Public railway lines shall not extend beyond the area under the jurisdiction of the respective provincial, municipal, or county government, except in special circumstances. Public railways may also raise private shares, but not exceeding 40% of the total assets. (3) The Dedicated Railway Regulations consist of 20 articles. Railways built exclusively for the transportation of the enterprise's own operations are called dedicated railways and shall be governed by these regulations. The above two articles are supplementary laws to the Railway Law. (Central News Agency Telegram, 18th)

(Nanjing) After the meeting on the 18th, Sun Ke summoned Chuan Bingchang and Wu Jingxiong and gave detailed instructions on the revision direction of the draft constitution. He also approved the request of Fu and Wu and sent a letter to Tao Lvqian, the former reviewer of the first draft of the constitution and the current Deputy Minister of Internal Affairs, to attend the review. At 2:00 p.m., Fu Bingchang, Wu Jingxiong, Wu Shangying, Liang Han Cao, Tao Lvqian, Lin Bin, He Sui, and others held a meeting in the lounge of the Yuan to begin the review. Ma Yinchu did not attend due to other matters. Fu Bingchang chaired the meeting. After the meeting adjourned at 4:30 p.m., Fu told reporters that the Central Government, in addition to promulgating the principles of revision, also issued an additional attachment stating that the attachment was based on five revision principles and made some revisions to the articles of the draft constitution, but they were incomplete. The meeting on the 18th had made a general revision of all the articles based on the principles promulgated by the Central Government and decided to hold another meeting on the afternoon of the 19th to make final concrete decisions and prepare a review report of the amendments to be submitted to President Sun for submission to the Yuan for deliberation. Fu also said that the five revision principles decided by the Central Government this time were indeed based on the strengths of the old and new constitutions and paid attention to "the substantialization of the articles of the constitution." As for the content of the five principles, it was not convenient to disclose them before the draft constitution amendment was passed. (Central News Agency Telegram, 18th)

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan held a meeting on the afternoon of the 18th to discuss and follow the five principles of the draft constitution passed by the Central Government and transferred for deliberation, preparing to undertake the amendment of the draft constitution. Internal Secretary Tao Lvqian was also invited to attend the discussion. Chairman Fu Bingchang heard that the discussion resulted in the completion of the research on the five principles transferred by the Central Government and decided to continue the meeting on the afternoon of the 19th to undertake the amendments, waiting for the full committee to discuss and pass them next Thursday before submitting them to the Central Government for special review. (Telegram, 18th)

Judicial Yuan Interprets Article 266 of the Criminal Law 58

(Nanjing) Xia Shirong, the prosecutor of Qu County, Zhejiang, telegraphed the Judicial Yuan, stating that Article 266 of the Criminal Law stipulates that those who gamble for money in public huts or places accessible to the public shall be fined up to 1,000 yuan, but this restriction does not apply to gambling with objects used for temporary entertainment. The second clause states that the gambling instruments and the money at the gambling table or exchange counters, whether belonging to the offender or not, shall be confiscated. According to legal interpretation, the "on the spot" in the second clause refers to the public huts or places accessible to the public mentioned in the first clause. Now, a certain Jia gambled at home and was raided by the Public Security Bureau. The gambling instruments and the gambling money on the gambling table were sent to the court for investigation. As it was not a public place or a hut accessible to the public, the gambling for money should not be punished according to law. The court decided not to prosecute. However, since Jia's act of gambling is not punishable, and the gambling instruments and gambling money were not seized in a public place or a place accessible to the public, can they still be regarded as contraband and confiscated? How should they be handled? Please interpret. The Judicial Yuan explained that the seized gambling instruments and gambling money are not contraband and cannot be confiscated separately. Since the decision has been made not to prosecute, Article 238, Section 2 of the Criminal Procedure Law should be followed. (Special Telegram, 18th)

Key Points of the Autopsy Examination Report on Xu Wansuzhen's Remains 65

(Nanjing) Liu Ruiheng, the Director of the Department of Health, issued a statement. The autopsy of Xu Wansuzhen's body began at 2:00 p.m. on the 15th, and the examination report was sent to the court on the evening of the 17th. The key points are as follows: (1) There were external injuries on the left side of the neck, head, and right thigh, but they were all abrasions and scratches and not fatal. (2) All organs of the body were free of disease. (3) The liver, kidneys, spleen, large intestine, and their contents were free of metallic and organic toxins. (4) There was no evidence of rape. (5) The important finding was that the blood inside the heart chambers and large blood vessels was not coagulated, and there was red blood. The autopsy was performed approximately 16 to 18 hours after her death. At this time, there should have been clots in the heart and blood vessels. This finding is consistent with death by suffocation. It is speculated that the deceased died within two to three hours after eating, as there was still a large amount of undigested food in the stomach. (Special Telegram, 18th)

Shandong: Break in the Dyke at Juancheng. The Situation at the Dongzhuang Mouth is About to Change Dramatically. Plans for Closing the Mouth are About to Change. 87

Jinan Correspondence: The situation at the dike in Juancheng has been tight for nearly a week. Qin Daoyu, the magistrate of Juancheng County, is leading more than 2,000 civilians in a desperate effort to reinforce the dike, fighting the Yellow River day and night. Pan Yifen, the engineering section chief of the River Affairs Bureau, and Chen Wenmo, the head of the upper reaches section, have also arrived to mobilize workers and materials to jointly protect the dike. However, the dangerous section is 100 zhang long, and the dike body has collapsed completely. Repairs are immediately lost. On the 16th, due to strong northwest winds, the Yellow River emptied and violently scoured the dike body, causing water seepage everywhere, making it impossible to block. At 8:30 AM on the 17th, a break occurred on the southern section. Officials and civilians retreated to the small embankment, increasing its height and thickness. It is still unknown whether it can be blocked. According to a telegram from Song Wentian, the chief engineer of the dike closure committee, the breach is 10 zhang wide and 3 chi deep. Zhang Lianjia, the director of the River Affairs Bureau, rushed from Kaifeng on the 17th, but it was too late. Han Fuju received a telegram from Qin Daoyu early on the 17th reporting the critical situation and replied that there was no need to worry and to do everything possible to protect it. After receiving the report of the breach, he still ordered Zhang Lianjia to supervise the protection. According to the observation of the dike closure committee, the Yellow River water is breaking through the Juancheng dike and flowing eastward, and in the future it may still enter the main river at Huanghuasi in the Huanghuasi, and the water leaking from the Dongzhuang Linpu mouth will inevitably decrease, or even silt up to become a dry mouth, which also cannot be known, the situation will inevitably change dramatically, the original plan for the dike closure project of the province, I am afraid it will change, and good supporting engineering will be more important, etc. The telegrams reporting the breach and the situation of the dam are recorded below.

Report Summary

(1) Limited to immediate arrival, to Zhang Junjian, Director of Jinan River Affairs Bureau, to be opened by Zhao Xunjian, Section Chief. I have wired a message to understand and look into it. From last night to this morning, six willow pillows have been pushed in, about 40 zhang long, and are being urgently added. About 2,000 civilians are distributed in the water overnight, working desperately to add sacks, but the working section is too long and the soil quality is too bad, and they collapse as soon as they are added, taking care of one but not the other, and they are overwhelmed. This morning at dawn, leaks appeared repeatedly, and after a desperate blockage, the water was not allowed to pass. Extending to 7:00, two more leaks appeared at the upper end, which were very violent. After blocking, they were strictly supervised by soldiers and rushed to block the water. After the blockage was completed, they were pursued and pressed with sacks, but the water flow was too fast to block. At 8:30, the embankment collapsed. We can only strictly supervise the soldiers to retreat to the small dam. However, since the dam is newly built and has not been weathered, and it is sandy soil, it is difficult to predict whether it can resist the water. Respectfully submitted by Qin Daoyu, Magistrate of Juancheng County, Chen Wenmo, Chief of the Upper Reaches Section, and Pan Yifen, Section Chief. (2) Briefly. I respectfully acknowledged the telegram. This morning, I set off from Kaifeng to investigate the collapse of the river banks at Tianhezui in the second section of southern Hebei Province and Lengzhai in the fourth section of the southern province, which are currently only twelve or thirteen zhang away. The bureau staff and soldiers are actively protecting them. If the water does not rise, there will be no danger for the time being. Arrived at Dongzhuang at 7:00 tonight. Respectfully reported by Zhang Lianjia (3) (Briefly) I humbly acknowledge it. At 9:00 this morning, Chen, Director of the Upper Reaches Section, reported by telephone from Duzhuang that the Juancheng civilian-built dam was not being maintained. Two villages were flooded. They are currently trying to protect the retreat, etc. discussed and submitted by Zhang Lianjia, Director of Shandong River Affairs Bureau. (4) Most Urgent. To Chairman Han of the Jinan Provincial Government, Juancheng dam has been rescued in vain for days, and collapsed through the water at 8:30 in the morning. We are now retreating to the pre-repaired small retreat dam and are working hard to increase its height and thickness. It is found that more than 20 sections of the dam have been repaired at the break, and they still have the effect of digging out the river. However, all the embankment cables are hanging and urgently need to be added. In addition to the River Affairs Bureau allocating straw materials, poles, and ropes to temporarily help with the rescue, please approve Juancheng's rescue fund of 10,000 to 20,000 yuan to increase public support and maintain important construction work. Zhang Lianjia (5) Urgent, to Zhang, Chairman of the Jinan Blockade Committee. According to reports, the Juancheng civilian dam has been opened, with a width of ten zhang and a water depth of three chi. The people are currently protecting the retreat dam. The current water level is falling day by day, and the retreat dam is easier to defend. Specially heard by Song Wentian.

Shape of the Dyke

The Yucheng Dyke is between the great dyke and the civilian dyke, initially built by the local people to prevent water leakage from the civilian dyke in the Lishengtun area and to protect the safety of the river loop. On the night of July 10 this year, the Lishengtun civilian dyke broke, and the water flowed south, breaking through the great dyke between Linpu and Dongzhuang, flooding western Shandong. Qin Daoyu, the magistrate of Juancheng County, feared that the river would roll eastward, endangering the river loop, so he led thousands of civilians to reinforce the Yucheng Dyke. At that time, the Yucheng Dyke was no more than five feet high and no more than one zhang wide. On the 11th, many loopholes were found. Qin Daoyu then requisitioned 30,000 civilians to repair it overnight, thickening and widening the dam. The base width was twelve zhang, the top width was three zhang six chi, and the height was one zhang two chi, thus becoming the only lifeline to protect the lives of hundreds of thousands of people in the river loop. Later, the current rolled eastward, the remaining dam collapsed, approaching the Yucheng Dyke, and there were repeated dangers. For the sake of safety, Qin Daoyu added a retreat dam behind the Yucheng Dyke, 580 zhang long, the base of the dam was four zhang wide, the top was one zhang five chi wide, and the height was eight chi. After that, the river's momentum was suddenly fast and slow, and for more than three months, there were rescue efforts from time to time. The public has exhausted their strength. Li Yizhi, the former chairman of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, once advocated that the Yucheng Dyke should be excavated to reduce the leakage from the mouth, making it easier to block. However, it was dismissed due to opposition from the people in the river loop. In the past month, the situation at the mouth has changed dramatically. The river water rushes out from the Lishengtun residual dike, passing through Daxiaoyanglou Wuzhuang to Xuzhuang, and has been brushed into a large east-west river channel, which is very smooth. The Yucheng Dyke was the first to bear the brunt. In the past week, the situation has become even more serious. More than 2,000 civilians have been working together to protect it. Qin Daoyu, the magistrate of Yucheng County, Pan Jianfen, the engineering section chief of the River Affairs Bureau, and Chen Wenmo, the head of the upper reaches section, have all arrived to help direct the work. In the end, it was difficult to change God's will, and it collapsed on the 17th. Although there is a retreat dyke behind it, according to general observation, the retreat dyke is soft and sandy and is difficult to resist. The water will inevitably flow eastward and will still follow the old course of the 14th year's breach and re-enter the main river at Huanghuasi in Shouzhang. Inside the river loop, in addition to the Yucheng county seat, there are more than 10,000 hectares of good farmland in Yuncheng, Fan County, Shouzhang, and other counties. (17th)

One of Shandong's Outstanding Cases: The Qingdao Guowu Farm. Recovered After Negotiations by the Municipal Government. More Than 15,000 Acres of Farmland. 88

Qingdao Correspondence: The Guowu Farm, operated by the Japanese in this city, is one of the outstanding cases in the detailed agreement for Shandong. Previous attempts to negotiate by each former standing committee ended without resolution due to the high prices demanded by the Japanese. Although this topic is small, it is of great importance to the integrity of our country's land administration. The current municipal authorities have repeatedly negotiated through assigned personnel, and as a result, the farmland has been completely recovered at a price of 81,000 yuan. The details are as follows:

The Origin of Guowu Farm

In the third year of the Republic of China (1914), after the Japanese occupied Qingdao, people from Japan rushed to the island to do business or farm. At that time, a certain Japanese person, taking advantage of the power of the Japanese government, forcibly bought land from the people in the Licun and Cangkou areas outside the city at the lowest price, ranging from dozens of yuan per mu. After the purchase, they were still rented to the original landlords for cultivation and rented annually. Later, a certain Japanese person sold the farmland to the Guowu Farm Company. This is the origin of Guowu Farm. In total, the farm bought about 15,873 mu of farmland before and after. When our country officially recovered Qingdao in December of the eleventh year of the Republic of China (1922), the Guowu Farm was also included in the detailed agreement for outstanding cases in Shandong. Item 4 of the supplement stipulates that "the Chinese government will recover the Guowu Farm and other large farms operated by the Japanese in the former German leased territory with fair compensation." In addition, it is noted that "details of the aforementioned recovery will be agreed upon by the Qingdao Commercial Bureau and the Japanese military officer."

The Process of Negotiating Recovery

Since our country recovered Qingdao, and the Guowu Farm was related to the issue of our country's land administration, negotiations could not be delayed. However, the Japanese initially demanded a staggering 10.4 million yuan. The municipal authorities were unable to proceed because of the excessive price. Therefore, negotiations with each past administration repeatedly stalled and yielded no results. The current mayor, Shen Honglie, recently sent Xie Zuyuan, the chief of the Municipal Government's Department No. 1, to negotiate repeatedly with the Japanese consul. After eleven years, this outstanding case was completely resolved this spring. Our side prepared a price of 81,000 yuan to recover all the farmland of the farm. Shen made a special gold commemorative medal for Xie's work on this case to reward him for his labor.

Renting After Recovery

After the municipal government recovered the farmland, the Finance Bureau stipulated that it be divided into three grades and still leased by the original landlords. The first grade is 200 yuan per mu, the second grade is 150 mu per mu, and the third grade is 100 yuan per mu. After all the farmland is released, a rent of 300,000 yuan can be obtained. However, it is heard that when the Japanese bought the land, they only gave dozens of yuan, and this time the lowest price released by the Finance Bureau is also more than 100 yuan. Therefore, many people are watching and waiting and are unwilling to lease. Recently, they also plan to jointly petition the municipal authorities to reduce the price in order to show sympathy.

Guangdong Province Issues Another 5 Million Yuan in Public Bonds to Fund Various Construction Projects 89

Recently, Guangdong Province has been enveloped in a general economic downturn. Commerce is far from what it used to be. At the same time, the rural economy is collapsing. In impoverished counties and areas that have suffered from natural disasters such as floods and droughts, the wealthy have declined, middle-class families can barely make ends meet, and those without permanent property are mostly destitute, or even die in ditches. For example, stores in Shanwei in Lufeng County and Southwest in Sanshui County have recently closed one after another. In the rural silk farms of Shunde County, the old and weak are crying for food. Those who can make a living can only get one full meal a day, and the rest are wrapped in coarse grains. The people are so poor that the exhaustion of rural finance can be seen. As a result, society and the business community are extremely depressed, and government tax revenues have also been greatly affected. The fiscal budget for the 24th year of the Republic (1935) is insufficient. Therefore, there is a resolution to pay administrative expenses at 80%. Although administrative expenses are paid at 80%, construction projects that should be carried out in the three-year plan must still be implemented. If we want to implement them, we must find ways to raise funds. Therefore, the government recently decided to raise public bonds and issue 5 million yuan of construction public bonds for various construction purposes. Last month, Chen Yuanzhen, manager of the Guangdong Provincial State-Owned Products Management Office, and Chen Zhongbi, president of the Guangzhou Municipal Bank, were sent to Beijing to discuss the construction public bond plan with the central financial authorities. When they passed through Shanghai, they also contacted the Shanghai financial community to discuss sales methods. The two Chens have already returned to Guangdong. It is said that this trip to Beijing and Shanghai has concrete methods for the issuance and sale of construction public bonds. As soon as the bonds are printed, they can be shipped to Shanghai for sale. The bonds are printed by the Shanghai Commercial Press and will be delivered in batches around the beginning of November. After the issuing agency signs and seals the bonds, they will be issued around the beginning of December. In the future, they will be sold in Guangdong and Shanghai, and if necessary, they will be distributed to various places in Beijing and Wuhan. Those who act as agents for sales will be given considerable benefits by the issuing agency to encourage them. These bonds are specifically used for construction, industry, and commerce in Guangdong Province, and a portion will be allocated to supplement the circulating funds of various state-owned factories. Detailed allocation will be specified one by one and must not be used for other purposes. (October 14)

Kunshan: The Eighth District Chief Requests Resignation 90

Cai Wuzai, the former standing committee member of the county party department, has made many achievements in local affairs since taking office as the district chief of the eighth district. Recently, due to poor health and heavy district affairs, he was unable to continue and submitted a request to the county government for resignation yesterday. Now, Magistrate Peng and the township chiefs of the district are doing their best to retain him.

Suzhou: Wanted Bandit Leader Chuan Lao Wuzi 91

The house of Zhu Yuanhe in Xuzhuang, Lujiang Township, outside the Zhaimen was robbed by bandits some time ago, and the hired worker was beaten to death by the bandits. The circumstances of the case have been reported in this newspaper. It is now known that two criminals, Shi Xiaodi and others, have been arrested and sent to the local procuratorate for interrogation. Shi Xiaodi and others have confessed to participating in the robbery, killing the hired worker, and using the loot. In addition to dispatching police to investigate and arrest him, the local procuratorate has also requested the Public Security Bureau to strictly arrest and handle the case.

Wuxi: Active Silk Market and Silkworm Cocoon Conditions 92

The spring silkworm harvest in Xiyi this year was good, and the silk reeling was excellent. In addition, the silk sales in Europe and the United States were active, and the silk market gradually rose. At present, it has reached 610 yuan, so the silk industry is showing signs of recovery. There are 41 factories operating in the whole city. However, the market situation for dry silkworm cocoons is strong. Southern goods require 250 yuan, and the prospects are still bullish. Northern goods are priced at 160 yuan, but there is a serious shortage of inventory. It is estimated that the current inventory of cocoons is only enough for the year. Once the spring begins, there will be no raw materials to make, and the demand for silk in Europe and the United States is still strong, and it seems that supply cannot meet demand. The reasons for this surge in sales are: (1) The European and American silk sales markets have long been monopolized by Japanese silk. This year, Japanese production has fallen sharply, and Chinese silk has been able to seize the opportunity to rise. (2) The American recovery movement has been effective, and the silk industry's operations have improved, and the demand for raw silk has increased, so sales have become increasingly prosperous. In addition, the silkworm breeding model area, in view of the rising silk sales and the lack of raw materials, is trying its best to promote the late autumn silkworm. More than 20,000 sheets of seeds have been issued. At first, due to the warm weather, the silkworms developed very well. Now, most of them have reached the stage of large hibernation and leaf opening, and the late ones are also in the third hibernation stage. However, the weather has changed drastically, with varying degrees of cold and warmth. Most of them have turned into white zombies with pus and empty heads. The harvest is expected to be only about 60%.

Jiangyin: Plans to Build a Road Along the North Waichang River 93

The riverbank from the north to Huangtiangang is a prosperous area for merchants from Jiangnan and Jiangbei. There is no road there, and the original embankment is narrow, and vehicles are crowded. At the county government affairs meeting on the 16th, County Magistrate Yan proposed that if a road is built from Junshan Park to the riverbank, merchants coming to Cheng from the upper and lower reaches of the river and from Jiangbei can also reach the city directly via Zhongshan Road. It was decided to first build the roadbed to facilitate traffic. The construction section will design it, prepare a budget, and submit it to the Construction Committee for review and handling.

Nantong: Mediation of Dispute Over Reclamation and Pastoral Land 94

Tonghai Reclamation and Pastoral Company donated 450 shares of land to the Tongzhou Normal School. The education community in Haimen disagreed. Later, the provincial government ruled that one-fifth, or 90 shares, should be given to Haimen. Haimen filed a lawsuit with the Executive Yuan, which was ruled by the Ministry of Education to maintain the original ruling of the Jiangsu Provincial Government. Haimen is still suing the Executive Yuan. Currently, people from Tonghai and Haimen counties are acting as mediators and will negotiate a solution in Shanghai in the coming days.

Pinghu　Zhapu Township Schools Entirely Strike 95

Each of the Zhapu Township-established schools, due to the educational authorities' accumulated debt of funds, with the least being over half a year and the most nearly a year, some have no means to repay debts, with school principals being waylaid and having their mandarin jackets stripped by shop staff; some principals, having exhausted all means, have attempted suicide by hanging; and the agricultural tax, due to embezzlement by collection staff who conceal and fail to remit, has already reached around 200,000 yuan. Besides detaining one or two collection staff, the county magistrate has no good way to recover the funds. On the 16th, the principals of each township school gathered to discuss that if this continues, their lives will be at stake. They jointly submitted their resignations to the county government, and from that day forward, notified the students' families to implement a strike.

Ningbo　Director of Navigation Administration Visits Ningbo for Inspection 96

Gao Ting, Director of the Navigation Administration Department of the Ministry of Transportation, arrived in Ningbo from Haimen on the 15th and stayed at the Hengtong Hotel on the north bank of the Ningbo River. Mingguang　Provincial Government Requests Disaster Relief for Anhui Northern Drought 97

The drought in various counties in northern Anhui is severe, surpassing the floods of the 20th year of the Republic in severity. Each county is successively appealing to the province for relief, but the provincial treasury is also strained, with no way to provide assistance. The provincial government has specifically telegraphed the Central Relief Commission, requesting the allocation of substantial funds to save the disaster-stricken populace. The original telegram is as follows: "The counties in northern Anhui Province have suffered a severe drought between summer and autumn, resulting in a failed harvest of millet and widespread misery. The drought disaster is extremely serious, even surpassing the floods along the Yangtze River this year. Urgent appeals for relief from various counties are pouring in, and Commissioner Xi Chulin has also come to the province to detail the disaster situation and plead for assistance. We are currently working with the province's disaster relief committee to find ways to provide relief. However, due to years of disasters and widespread hardship, even with our best efforts, fundraising efforts are insufficient to meet the severe disaster. We earnestly request your committee to consider the extraordinary severity of the drought in northern Anhui and swiftly allocate substantial funds for disaster relief."

Kamekichi Takahashi Came to Shanghai to Research New Policies Towards China; Gave a Talk to Japanese Reporters 105

The Japanese Shanghai Daily News reports that Kamekichi Takahashi, Director of the Economic Research Institute, arrived in Shanghai on the Nagasaki Maru at 3:30 PM on the 17th, accompanied by his staff member Aoyama Jiro, to explore guidelines for new economic policies towards China. He plans to visit economic cities such as Hong Kong, Guangzhou, Hankou, Qingdao, Jinan, and Tianjin over a period of forty days to conduct on-site investigations of the current state of the economy, in order to provide a reference for the Japanese government's new economic policies towards China. Takahashi made the following remarks to Japanese reporters on the ship: "The government's China policy has already become a problem. How exactly to determine the recent economic policy towards China requires on-site research. The materials obtained from various locations will be used as a guideline for implementation. Originally, China-Japan economic cooperation was based on the changes in the world's political and economic situation. Adjusting China-Japan relations, the so-called China-Japan relations in the era of free economy are very different from the current era of closed economy, so it should be considered carefully," and so on.

Aviation Society Begins Recruiting Members; Divided into Three Types with the Goal of 6,000 Members; Elementary Flying Class to be Established After Quota is Met 106

The Central News Agency reports that the China Aviation Society, after announcing its establishment on the 10th of this month, is now recruiting members and actively proceeding. It is reported that after recruiting 6,000 members, an elementary flying class will be established to popularize aviation knowledge and flying skills. According to Mr. Zhu, the person in charge of the society, speaking to reporters, the details are as follows:

Recruitment

The Aviation Society's current recruitment of members is progressing smoothly. Members are divided into three types: Regular members, who have aviation expertise and skills, such as current pilots or mechanics, and graduates of aviation schools, who are introduced into the society by various organizations, companies, and schools. Many people have already come from Beijing, Hangzhou, and other places to contact the society. Special members are those who are enthusiastic supporters and donate funds, who are invited into the society by the society. Ordinary members, who are currently being publicly recruited, are those who aspire to learn to fly or are interested in aviation academia and sympathize with the society's goals, and can fill out an application form to officially join the society.

Purpose

The recruitment goal is to establish an elementary flying class after 6,000 members have been recruited. Members who have already studied and those who have not can join flying. Members in the society will assist or coach, giving those who have studied the convenience of practice and those who have not the opportunity to learn. After completing 15 hours of initial flight training and passing the examination, they will graduate and be issued a certificate by the government, recognizing them as elementary first-level pilots, who are standing members of the national aviation force. Mr. Zhu concluded by saying that he hopes that young people across the country will enthusiastically engage in this emerging air sport, in order to popularize aviation education and cultivate aviation talent.

Regulations

1. These regulations are formulated in accordance with Chapters II and IV of the China Aviation Society's constitution. 2. The types of members and fees of the society are as follows: A. Annual membership fees: (1) Regular members: annual regular fee of 2 yuan; (2) Ordinary members: annual regular fee of 5 yuan; (3) Special members: annual donation of 50 yuan or more. B. One-time donations: (1) Special members: one-time donation of 200 yuan or more. C. Flight training fees: (1) Regular members: in addition to the society assigning instructors to provide voluntary assistance, fees are charged per hour according to the amount of fuel consumed; (2) Ordinary members: the first phase of flight training is 15 hours, with a fee of 600 yuan. Academic subjects and practical training are all taught voluntarily. The cost of flight suits, etc., will be determined separately; (3) Special members are the same as regular members. (3) Membership procedures (A) Fill out a membership application form and pay the membership fee, and submit it to the society's general affairs department to issue a receipt; (B) Regular members must submit verification of graduation certificates from aviation institutions and flight certificates or mechanical certificates; (C) Ordinary members who wish to practice first-level flying must first have the qualifications of that member and follow the first phase admission procedures (detailed admission regulations will be formulated separately); (D) Special members fill out a membership application form and submit the donation fee to the society's general affairs department to issue a receipt; (E) Ordinary members who pass the second phase graduation examination can be promoted to regular members.

Rights and Responsibilities

(1) The society's purposes are: (A) to popularize aviation knowledge and technology; (B) to establish a national spirit of fearlessness; (C) to cultivate an aviation enthusiasm; (D) to promote an interest in flying; (2) The society, in response to the needs of the times, opens up new paths for the lives of young men and women compatriots and assists the government in developing private aviation; (3) The society is a place for enthusiastic and aspiring aviation practitioners to conduct joint research and is not of a commercial nature; (4) In order to facilitate regular members, in addition to sufficient practice flying at the society's airfield, long-distance flights can be made to various locations as appropriate (5) Special members, regardless of whether they have studied or are beginners, the society can send personnel to assist in flying. The flight procedures for the above four and five clauses will be determined separately; (6) All members of the society, when taking domestic commercial aviation routes, the society can negotiate on their behalf to enjoy discounted rates; (7) All members of the society can enjoy discounted sightseeing flights of the society. Regulations for sightseeing flights will be determined separately; (8) Ordinary members of the society who graduate from the first level and pass the examination will have their certificates issued by the government upon application by the society, recognizing them as elementary first-level pilots; (9) All members of the society can enjoy the right to read the society's publications for free; (10) The society invites Chinese and foreign aviation experts to lecture on the progress of the aviation era. All members of the society can participate for free; (11) All members of the society have priority in participating in various aviation sports organizations that the society has held and plans to hold.

Cotton Adulteration with Water and Impurities Slightly Restrained; Suppression Work Has Achieved Considerable Results 107

The Central News Agency reports that because ordinary cotton farmers and merchants covet meager profits, the practice of adulterating cotton with water and impurities has been prevalent. Since the National Government promulgated the Provisional Regulations for Suppressing Adulteration of Cotton with Water and Impurities and its implementing rules last year, the Central Cotton Adulteration Suppression Office of the National Economic Council's Cotton Industry Control Committee was established, and joint Cotton Adulteration Suppression Offices in Shaanxi, Henan, Shandong, and Hubei provinces were formed with the construction departments of the four provinces. The heads of the construction departments of each province concurrently serve as directors to implement investigations and inspections. The work of each office has now reached one year. Reporters visited the person in charge of the Central Cotton Adulteration Suppression Office and learned that each suppression office has been able to handle the inspection of cotton conscientiously. All cases that have been discovered have been strictly dealt with according to the law. As a result, the practice of adulterating cotton with water and impurities has been slightly restrained. The following is an excerpt of the major cases of punishment for adulteration with water and impurities: 1. The Jiading District sub-office of Jiangsu Province discovered a certain flower shop and ginner in Taicang, Sha Creek, and transferred the case to the Taicang County government, which also handles judicial affairs, and sentenced the manager of the shop to a fine of 250 yuan and two months of detention. In addition, the Nantong District sub-office discovered an agent of a yarn factory transporting cotton with impurities, and sent him to the Changshu County government, which sentenced him to a fine of 100 yuan. 2. The Zheng County sub-office of Henan Province discovered a batch of cotton adulterated by cotton merchant Zhang and sent it to the county government, which fined him 300 yuan. The Shan County sub-office discovered a batch of cotton adulterated with water by a certain flower shop and sent it to the county government, which sentenced it to a fine of 800 yuan and three months of imprisonment. In addition, the Luo County sub-office discovered a batch of cotton adulterated with water by a certain flower shop and sent it to the county government, which sentenced it to a fine of 400 yuan. 3. The Weinan sub-office of Shaanxi Province discovered that a batch of cotton adulterated by cotton merchant Wang was sentenced by the county government to a fine of 100 yuan, or 100 days of imprisonment in lieu of payment. The Jingyang sub-office discovered that a certain flower shop's re-examined cotton was unqualified and sent it to the county government for a fine. 4. The First District sub-office of Hubei Province discovered a batch of cotton adulterated by a certain flower shop and sent it to the Guanghua County government, which sentenced it to a fine of 1,000 yuan. In addition, the office discovered that a batch of cotton adulterated by cotton merchant Xu was sentenced by the Guanghua County government to one year of imprisonment. The moisture and impurity content of Chinese cotton has indeed gradually decreased in recent years. The following is a comparison table of the highest and lowest percentages of moisture and impurities in Chinese cotton over the past two years for reference.

Decisions from the South District Rent Reduction Meeting: No Rent Reduction, No Rent Payment; All Deposits in Banks Starting October; Branch Associations in All Areas Limited to One Month to Organize 112

According to New Voice Society, the Nanshi District Rent Reduction Committee has established over 200 branch associations since its establishment last year. Besides those that have reached settlements, over 100 are still working hard. Therefore, representatives of shops and residents in Nanshi, such as Shen Xinfu, stated that while a few active branch associations have achieved rent reductions again and again, those who do not understand the procedures or act alone in requesting rent reductions not only fail to obtain rent reductions but also win themselves lawsuits. This is not beneficial to society in the long run. Therefore, on the 16th, they held a representative meeting of the Nanshi district's businesses and residents' rent reduction movement at the Shaonian Yi Jiang Guan, proposing to promote the establishment of rent reduction branch associations in all lanes and blocks of Nanshi within one month. Before obtaining a clear order from the Sixth Plenary Session, the following items will be temporarily implemented. After being approved by the entire meeting, it was submitted to the South District Rent Reduction Committee for implementation. The committee specially invited representatives from the city's rent reduction efforts yesterday afternoon. Attendees included Zheng Jianbo, Standing Committee Member of the Joint Rent Reduction Association of Various Districts; Hu Yibo, Standing Committee Member of the Zhabei District; Zhang Binghua, Standing Committee Member of the Pudong District Association; Zhu Wenbo, Standing Committee Member of the Huxi District Association; and Shen Xingu, Executive Committee Member of the Nanshi District, and over 50 others. Shen Xinfu, Zhu Tiwu, and Yang Qiqing were publicly elected as the presidium. After performing the rituals, the following matters were discussed: (1) Resolutions submitted by the representative meeting of businesses and residents in the Nanshi district. It stated that although rent reductions, both voluntary and involuntary, are heard of daily in the Nanshi District, the problem has not been thoroughly resolved. How should it be promoted to complete the universal rent reduction plan? Resolution: Send a letter to the South District Rent Reduction Committee, requesting it to send representatives to participate in the Shanghai City Rent Reduction Petition Group and go to Beijing to petition the Sixth Plenary Session. Before obtaining a clear order, the South District Committee will notify all branch associations in the South District to follow the following resolutions: (1) Each rent reduction association will investigate each household. Those who have not yet organized must organize within one month. (2) All disputes or lawsuits arising from rent reduction issues before this meeting should be reported to the local rent reduction association for legal assistance. (3) Those who feel that the rent is high and request a reduction must not default on rent due to rent increases before a resolution is reached. Rent arrears before October are not subject to this rule. Starting from October, all rent payments should be suspended, and the rent should be deposited in a bank. The methods and procedures will be designated by each association for handling. (4) If second landlords profit from leases and undermine rent reductions, subtenants within the same address may jointly request rent reductions and lower rents. (5) In this economic downturn, with the fall in commodity prices, reducing rent is an urgent matter. When initiating rent reductions in various areas, residents must not obstruct or resist the overall resolution due to kinship or friendship with the landlord. If the above facts occur, it should be submitted to the assembly for punishment. (6) Those who request rent reductions without the regulations of the Rent Reduction Committee and the resolutions of the plenary meeting of each location, and act alone, thereby hindering the overall interests, all overall losses should be fully compensated by the individual acting alone. The resolutions were duly recorded and approved for strict implementation. (2) Report on the housing case of Liang Yi Fang in Xicang. After investigation by this committee, the rent is indeed higher than the surrounding areas. Although the landlord has already expressed a 10% discount, it is still not fair. A resolution should be requested. Resolution: Send a letter to the landlord, requesting him to express to the tenants within five days that he will voluntarily reduce the rent by 20%, otherwise, according to the tenants' wishes, permission is granted to suspend payment and file a lawsuit. Approved. (3) Resolution on determining the address of the Nanshi District Association of the Rent Reduction Joint Association. Resolved: Temporarily at Wu An Elementary School, Qinglian Street, Nine Acre Land. (4) The branches of Minguo Road, Xinhua Road, Fangbang Road, and Zhaojiabang Road are requested to hire lawyers Zhou Lianze, Zhu Yakui, and Wang Liwu as legal advisors to the branches. Resolution passed. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

National Goods Groups Collect Samples of Products 113

Xia Pu County, Fujian Province, in order to promote national goods, has launched the establishment of a national goods exhibition hall and sent a letter to the China General Federation of Industry requesting it to collect products on its behalf. The federation has sent letters to its members and factories, stating: "With the opening of seaports after the White Opium War, foreign goods flooded in, absorbing cash. Not only has the commercial arena suffered, but it has also affected rural bankruptcy. In recent years, national goods have been exquisitely made, practical, and affordable. Compared with imported goods, they are no less inferior. However, they have failed to reduce the record-breaking surplus of customs. The reason is that consumers do not recognize national goods and misuse foreign goods, and producers fail to publicize their goods to the best of their ability. As a result, even with national goods, foreign goods are still used, or due to traffic obstruction, the supply and demand of production from various places cannot be balanced. There is a surplus of national products here, and similar foreign goods are used there. In view of this, the Association plans to organize a national goods exhibition, sending separate letters to major domestic factories, soliciting samples or specimens of various products, in order to promote them. We know that your association is the highest industrial organization in the country, so we hereby send this letter and request you to check and forward the purpose of our association to your members, and we hope that you will provide us with samples or specimens of various products, indicating the type, price, month, and description as much as possible. We will widely introduce and publicize them, and we look forward to your reply." According to the meeting, a corresponding letter was issued immediately, and it was announced that it should be checked, verified, and sent to the Association for collection and transfer. The matter concerns one's own interests and should not be delayed. The China National Products Manufacturers Association yesterday notified all its members and factories, saying: "For the purpose of notification, according to a letter from the China Youth Using National Goods, 'Since the opening of our country to the sea, due to the decline of industry, countless amounts of money have flowed out every year, resulting in great economic difficulties for the people. In recent years, although the authorities and those concerned about national affairs have regarded the huge amount of money flowing out as sufficient to harm the country, they have spared no effort in promoting national goods. However, our country has a vast territory, and there are many places with inconvenient transportation, and cooperation between production and sales is difficult to popularize. The colleagues of our group, in view of this, plan to go to all parts of the country and to the residences of overseas Chinese in Nanyang to expand publicity, with areas with inconvenient transportation as important publicity sites. The publicity method is to hold exhibitions of national product samples in various places, and to collect samples in various places, introduce each other, and investigate the sources and specialties of all daily necessities of the people in various places, for the research and adoption of industrialists. However, at the beginning of the process, we must rely on the guidance of national goods groups and industrial experts. We are responsible for being the leading agency in the national goods industry, and we should be fully aware of the national goods factories. For the convenience of collection, we specially send this letter to your association to collect samples of completely national goods, so that they can be taken to various places to introduce to the public, and to provide guidance.'" Accordingly, it is hereby notified that if manufacturers wish to have the group introduce them, please send samples to the association immediately, and indicate the capital, the source of raw materials, the manufacturing situation, whether Chinese workers are employed, the purpose, and the history of the enterprise, so that they can be collected and handed over to the group to be taken to various places for publicity. The Telephone Company Does Not Cancel Toll Fees, Two Reasons Are Difficult to Establish 115

Both Parties Can Re-Negotiate the Contract, and the Lines Can be Re-equipped.

If the Interests of the Public Are Taken into Account, Cancellation Should Be Expedited

The Shanghai Telephone Company in the concession, in response to opposition from all parties to the five-cent toll fee, requested the cancellation of the fee. The company specially issued two reasons for not canceling it: (1) Due to the temporary telephone contract, it is not convenient to change it midway, and this toll fee must continue to be collected. (2) Due to the different structures of the two-way automatic telephone exchanges, it is not convenient to dial directly, and the current manual switching method must continue to be used. A reporter from New Voice Xiang consulted relevant parties for their opinions, and they expressed the following: (1) The temporary telephone contract was signed by the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities, the Ministry of Transportation Shanghai Telephone Bureau, and the Shanghai Telephone Company. The current Telephone Bureau and the Bureau of Public Utilities, for the convenience of public transportation, both advocate the cancellation of this toll fee. This has been reported in various newspapers. Furthermore, the Telephone Bureau has already provided telephone users with 40 free calls per month for Type A users and 80 free calls per month for Type B users. If the Shanghai Telephone Company can also take public interests as a premise, then with the consent of both parties, this toll fee can be cancelled. (2) The automatic switch installed by the Shanghai Telephone Company is a rotary type, and the automatic switch installed by the Shanghai Telephone Bureau is a step-by-step type. Although the structures of the two switches are incompatible, a changing machine line can be added between the two-way lines to replace the current manual station. Then, users of both parties can dial directly. Moreover, the manual station requires hiring drivers. If direct dialing is used, this expense can be saved. After the improvement, not only will the public benefit, but the company and the Telephone Bureau themselves will also be able to save more on the monthly expenses required to maintain the calls. The Ministry of Transportation Shanghai Telephone Bureau and the Shanghai Telephone Company in the concession have repeatedly discussed the cancellation of the five-cent toll fee in the Chinese concession. However, because the telephone company used the telephone contract and the different machines as excuses, no concrete measures were taken. Chinese users have also requested the Bureau to realize the cancellation as soon as possible because the Telephone Bureau has not been able to completely cancel the fee.

According to Dagong News Agency, the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation plans to promote the development of rural economic prosperity in several provinces such as Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, and Jiangxi, and has successively established loan agencies in Kunshan, Wujiang, and other counties to handle various loans and pledges for agricultural products and rural side businesses in order to regulate the economy. The Ministry of Industry Asks the Municipal Government to Ban the Sale of Water-Containing Damp Tea; A Reward Will Be Granted for Moisture Content Below 30 Percent 123

The Shanghai Municipal Government received a notice from the Ministry of Industry, Commerce No. 37567, stating that the letter from the Secretariat of the National Economic Commission, "The plan of the Commission to revive the tea industry originally included improving the quality of tea. In recent years, Chinese tea has always had a burnt taste, which has led to a sharp decline in quality. It is often criticized when sold, and the price is low. The most taboo of tea is the burnt taste, which has a great impact on the sales of tea. The reason for the burnt taste is that the raw tea contains too much water. Therefore, the sale of damp tea should be strictly prohibited. It is proposed that the Grand Office send a letter to the Ministry of Industry, ordering all tea-producing provinces in the country to strictly prohibit damp tea. The sale of any raw tea with a water content exceeding 45% should be prohibited, and a reward should be granted for moisture content below 30%." The letter also stated, "Please submit the letter for review and handling. In addition to replying to the letter and sending copies, please also consult with the responsible officials and ask them to comply."

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Asks the Ministry of Finance to Pay Attention to the Case of Rough Stone Penalties at Customs; Cases Where Penalties Have Been Executed Are Penalized Again; There is No Such Law, Whether Criminal or Administrative Penalties 124

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce submitted a letter to the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating: "In the matter of the request, on the 3rd of this month, this Association received a directive from the Ministry's Customs Letter No. 7307, stating that the General Taxation Department had submitted a reply on the handling of the Chen Kaiqing Rough Stone case in Shanghai Customs, and a copy of the original submission was attached. It was ordered to be informed, etc. When the Association received the original submission, it forwarded it to Chen Kaiqing for information. Now, it is learned that the merchant has forwarded a copy of the objection submitted to Customs, requesting assistance. As this case has been submitted by the merchant to Shanghai Customs, it is not necessary to submit a direct appeal to the Ministry at this time, procedurally speaking. However, there is one crucial point in this case that must be stated. Chen Kaiqing's rough stones transported to Shanghai for sale are no more than the scope of underreporting the price, as stated in the sections submitted by the General Taxation Department. In other words, it is only one case. According to the principle that one matter should not be tried again, the case has been executed. After the execution is completed, a new penalty is imposed, regardless of whether it is a criminal penalty or an administrative penalty. There is no such law, which opens a precedent that has never existed before. The imported goods that have been taxed and released as cited in the original submission of Shanghai Customs can still be inspected by Customs at any time, which is also inappropriate. This clause clearly states that the goods that have been taxed can still be inspected at any time, not that the case that has been punished and completed can still be inspected and penalized. The two situations are different and should not be compared in a crooked way. In short, in the Chen Kaiqing case, the various arguments in the objection letter are a clarification of the facts, and the Association need not say much. The principle of not trying a matter again must not be destroyed by any means. Otherwise, the rights of the people will always be in an uncertain position. This is the main point of the case and must be brought to the attention of the Ministry. As for the disposition issued by Shanghai Customs, no reason for the disposition was given. If the merchant had not received the copy of the submission forwarded by the Association, it would have been impossible to raise an objection. This is another example of Shanghai Customs' failure to fully comply with the legal procedures. It is appropriate to attach a copy of the original objection letter and present it for the review of the Ministry.

Italy Eagerly Needs Eggs; Chinese Factories Have No Goods to Supply: Increased Exports are Not Credible 132

According to the Guowen News Agency, previous reports stated that Chinese egg factories, due to the tense relationship between Italy and Abyssinia in Europe, Italian merchants specially purchased eggs in China for shipment to Italy, resulting in a large export of Chinese dried eggs. Yesterday, reporters inquired about this with egg industry and egg merchant circles in Shanghai. According to manufacturers familiar with the industry, there are many Chinese egg factories, but the largest exporters are Tianjin, Shanghai, and Hankou, followed by Qingdao. The dried eggs, dried egg yolks, dried egg whites, and frozen egg yolks produced by egg factories are mostly produced in the spring. In the autumn, fresh eggs are in greater demand by residents in the interior, and egg prices increase, so egg factories generally stop production during this period. The goods sold overseas are those produced in the spring for sale. Normally, nine-tenths are sold to the United States, and the rest are sold to Europe. As for Italy, the quantity is very small. This year, due to the Italo-Abyssinian War, Italy urgently needs eggs, but Chinese egg factories can be said to have no goods to supply. As a result, the price of dried egg yolks alone has increased by about one-tenth due to the lack of goods, and the export volume is not large. Exports from Shanghai are even less than those from Tianjin. In short, in recent years, exporters have found it increasingly difficult to export Chinese eggs due to high tariffs and increased costs. The previous rumor that Qinhuangdao intended to use ships to transport Chinese eggs for export, and that egg products from Tianjin and Shanghai were increasing exports, is not credible.

Global Catholic Church Holds Mission Day: Shanghai Catholic Churches Will Expand Publicity Tomorrow 133

The third Sunday of every October (i.e., tomorrow) is the Catholic Church's Global Mission Day. On this day, universal believers assist in the promotion of missionary work through three methods: prayer, publicity, and donations. This year, Archbishop Salotti, President of the Society for the Propagation of the Faith, will deliver a broadcast speech in multiple languages on the Vatican Radio Station. Anyone in the world with a shortwave radio can hear it. The first broadcast will be at 6:00 PM on Saturday, the 19th, with a wavelength of 19.84 meters. The second broadcast will be at 2:40 AM on Sunday, the 20th (all Shanghai time), with a wavelength of 50.26 meters. All Catholic churches in the city have been ordered by Bishop Hu to conduct expanded official publicity tomorrow. In addition to religious ceremonies, donations will be collected at the entrances of various churches to help the poor and disaster-stricken missionary areas. The Catholic Church on Nansun Road in Hongkou will also have a donation group composed of Chinese, British, American, Portuguese, French, and Japanese young ladies collecting donations in front of the church. The Yangjingbang Catholic Action Association issued an official statement as follows:

It has been nineteen centuries since our Lord Jesus completed the great work of redemption. Although the Holy Church has relied on the tireless efforts of the apostles, bishops, and priests, who have crossed mountains and seas, undeterred by dangers, it has reaped rich harvests. Thanks to the sweat and blood of many heroic missionaries, the gospel of salvation has spread to the five continents. However, most people have not yet heard the gospel, and even entire nations are immersed in the darkness of foreign religions. Therefore, the souls of hundreds of millions of people cannot be redeemed, and the precious blood of the Savior seems to have been shed in vain for them. Now, missionaries around the world, more than 19,000 priests, more than 9,000 assistant brothers, and more than 51,000 nuns, constantly appeal to us from the vast missionary areas, asking us to replenish their strength so that they can advance the cause of the church and save many souls, sharing in the grace of redemption. We must know that in order to cultivate native clergy, a lot of funds are needed. Those who preach the gospel also need a minimum of living expenses. The construction and maintenance costs of all churches, schools, hospitals, nurseries, orphanages, and homes for the elderly are also very large. These funds are received by the Pontifical Society for the Propagation of the Faith from offerings from believers around the world, and after centralized control, they are distributed to various missionary areas. If the organization lacks generous donations from believers and donations decrease day by day, then the missionary fund loses its guarantee, and tens of thousands of missionaries lack assistance, and the cause is difficult to develop, and may even have to stop. The current Pope said that as long as one missionary is forced to stop working because he cannot get the economic assistance we can provide, it is a major responsibility. Therefore, on this annual Mission Day, we must generously donate to meet the material needs of the missionaries, and in our prayers, in the Mass, and after receiving Holy Communion, we must fervently pray for the missionary cause, so that there will be abundant harvests, the Holy Church will flourish, and the Kingdom of the Lord will come to the world.

Although her spirit is numb, she sometimes cries out in pain, so there is no danger to her life. It was also said that his wife was almost overwhelmed with grief after arriving in Shanghai. The funeral has been scheduled for 10:00 AM this morning. As for where he will be buried in the future, it has not been considered yet. As for the duties of Dasheng Cotton Mill and Dada Company, they are currently being handled by agents, and all matters will not be suspended as a result. (Guowen News Agency)
